\t// BloomStore is a dependency of IndexGateway and Bloom Planner & Builder.\n775: \t// Do not instantiate store and do not create a service if neither ar enabled.\n776: \tif !t.Cfg.BloomGateway.Enabled && !t.Cfg.BloomBuild.Enabled {\n777: \t\treturn nil, nil\n778: \t}\n779: \n780: \tif !config.UsingObjectStorageIndex(t.Cfg.SchemaConfig.Configs) {\n781: \t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"not using shipper index type\")\n782: \t}\n783: \n784: \tt.updateConfigForShipperStore()\n785: \n786: \tvar err error\n787: \tlogger := log.With(util_log.Logger, \"component\", \"bloomstore\")\n788: \n789: \treg := prometheus.DefaultRegisterer\n790: \tbsCfg := t.Cfg.StorageConfig.BloomShipperConfig\n791: \n792: \tvar metasCache cache.Cache\n793: \tif t.Cfg.isTarget(IndexGateway) && cache.IsCacheConfigured(bsCfg.MetasCache) {\n794: \t\tmetasCache, err = cache.New(bsCfg.MetasCache, reg, logger, stats.BloomMetasCache, constants.Loki)\n795: \n796: \t\t// always enable LRU cache\n797: \t\tlruCfg := bsCfg.MetasLRUCache\n798: \t\tlruCfg.Enabled = true\n799: \t\tlruCfg.PurgeInterval = 1 * time.Minute\n800: \t\tlruCache := cache.NewEmbeddedCache(\"inmemory-metas-lru\", lruCfg, reg, logger, stats.BloomMetasCache)\n801: \n802: \t\tmetasCache = cache.NewTiered([]cache.Cache{lruCache, metasCache})\n803: \t\tif err != nil {\n804: \t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create metas cache: %w\", err)\n805: \t\t}\n806: \t} else {\n807: \t\tlevel.Info(logger).Log(\"msg\", \"no metas cache configured\")\n808: \t}\n809: \n810: \tblocksCache := bloomshipper.NewFsBlocksCache(bsCfg.BlocksCache, reg, logger)\n811: \tif err = bloomshipper.LoadBlocksDirIntoCache(bsCfg.WorkingDirectory, blocksCache, logger); err != nil {\n812: \t\tlevel.Warn(logger).Log(\"msg\", \"failed to preload blocks cache\", \"err\", err)\n813: \t}\n814: \n815: \tvar pageAllocator mempool.Allocator\n816: \n817: \t// Set global BloomPageAllocator variable\n818: \tswitch bsCfg.MemoryManagement.BloomPageAllocationType {\n819: \tcase \"simple\":\n820: \t\tpageAllocator = &mempool.SimpleHeapAllocator{}\n821: \tcase \"dynamic\":\n822: \t\t// sync buffer pool for bloom pages\n823: \t\t// 128KB 256KB 512KB 1MB 2MB 4MB 8MB 16MB 32MB 64MB 128MB\n824: \t\tpageAllocator = mempool.NewBytePoolAllocator(128<<10, 128<<20, 2)\n825: \tcase \"fixed\":\n826: \t\tpageAllocator = mempool.New(\"bloom-page-pool\", bsCfg.MemoryManagement.BloomPageMemPoolBuckets, reg)\n827: \tdefault:\n828: \t\t// should not happen as the type is validated upfront\n829: \t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create bloom store: invalid allocator type\")\n830: \t}\n831: \n832: \tt.BloomStore, err = bloomshipper.NewBloomStore(t.Cfg.SchemaConfig.Configs, t.Cfg.StorageConfig, t.ClientMetrics, metasCache, blocksCache, pageAllocator, reg, logger)\n833: \tif err != nil {\n834: \t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create bloom store: %w\", err)\n835: \t}\n836: \n837: \treturn services.NewIdleService(nil, func(_ error) error {\n838: \t\tt.BloomStore.Stop()\n839: \t\treturn nil\n840: \t}), nil\n841: }\n842: \n843: func (t *Loki) updateConfigForShipperStore() {\n844: \t// Always set these configs\n845: \tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.BoltDBShipperConfig.IndexGatewayClientConfig.Mode = t.Cfg.IndexGateway.Mode\n846: \tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.TSDBShipperConfig.IndexGatewayClientConfig.Mode = t.Cfg.IndexGateway.Mode\n847: \n848: \tif t.Cfg.IndexGateway.Mode == indexgateway.RingMode {\n849: \t\tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.BoltDBShipperConfig.IndexGatewayClientConfig.Ring = t.indexGatewayRingManager.Ring\n850: \t\tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.TSDBShipperConfig.IndexGatewayClientConfig.Ring = t.indexGatewayRingManager.Ring\n851: \t}\n852: \n853: \tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.BoltDBShipperConfig.IngesterName = t.Cfg.Ingester.LifecyclerConfig.ID\n854: \tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.TSDBShipperConfig.IngesterName = t.Cfg.Ingester.LifecyclerConfig.ID\n855: \n856: \t// If RF > 1 and current or upcoming index type is boltdb-shipper then disable index dedupe and write dedupe cache.\n857: \t// This is to ensure that index entries are replicated to all the boltdb files in ingesters flushing replicated data.\n858: \tif t.Cfg.Ingester.LifecyclerConfig.RingConfig.ReplicationFactor > 1 {\n859: \t\tt.Cfg.ChunkStoreConfig.DisableIndexDeduplication = true\n860: \t\tt.Cfg.ChunkStoreConfig.WriteDedupeCacheConfig = cache.Config{}\n861: \t}\n862: \n863: \tswitch true {\n864: \tcase t.Cfg.isTarget(Ingester), t.Cfg.isTarget(Write):\n865: \t\t// Use embedded cache for caching index in memory, this also significantly helps performance.\n866: \t\tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.IndexQueriesCacheConfig = cache.Config{\n867: \t\t\tEmbeddedCache: cache.EmbeddedCacheConfig{\n868: \t\t\t\tEnabled:   true,\n869: \t\t\t\tMaxSizeMB: 200,\n870: \t\t\t\t// This is a small hack to save some CPU cycles.\n871: \t\t\t\t// We check if the object is still valid after pulling it from cache using the IndexCacheValidity value\n872: \t\t\t\t// however it has to be deserialized to do so, setting the cache validity to some arbitrary amount less than the\n873: \t\t\t\t// IndexCacheValidity guarantees the Embedded cache will expire the object first which can be done without\n874: \t\t\t\t// having to deserialize the object.\n875: \t\t\t\tTTL: t.Cfg.StorageConfig.IndexCacheValidity - 1*time.Minute,\n876: \t\t\t},\n877: \t\t}\n878: \n879: \t\t// We do not want ingester to unnecessarily keep downloading files\n880: \t\tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.BoltDBShipperConfig.Mode = indexshipper.ModeWriteOnly\n881: \t\tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.BoltDBShipperConfig.IngesterDBRetainPeriod = shipperQuerierIndexUpdateDelay(t.Cfg.StorageConfig.IndexCacheValidity, t.Cfg.StorageConfig.BoltDBShipperConfig.ResyncInterval)\n882: \n883: \t\tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.TSDBShipperConfig.Mode = indexshipper.ModeWriteOnly\n884: \t\tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.TSDBShipperConfig.IngesterDBRetainPeriod = shipperQuerierIndexUpdateDelay(t.Cfg.StorageConfig.IndexCacheValidity, t.Cfg.StorageConfig.TSDBShipperConfig.ResyncInterval)\n885: \n886: \tcase t.Cfg.isTarget(Querier), t.Cfg.isTarget(Ruler), t.Cfg.isTarget(Read), t.Cfg.isTarget(Backend), t.isModuleActive(IndexGateway), t.Cfg.isTarget(BloomPlanner), t.Cfg.isTarget(BloomBuilder):\n887: \t\t// We do not want query to do any updates to index\n888: \t\tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.BoltDBShipperConfig.Mode = indexshipper.ModeReadOnly\n889: \t\tt.Cfg.StorageConfig.TSDBShipperConfig.Mode = indexshipper.ModeReadOnly\n890: \n891: \tdefault:\n892: \t\t// All other targets use the shipper store in RW mode\n893: [line truncated]\n2: \n3: HttpRouter is a lightweight high performance HTTP request router (also called *multiplexer* or just *mux* for short) for [Go](https://golang.org/).\n4: \n5: In contrast to the [default mux](https://golang.org/pkg/net/http/#ServeMux) of Go's `net/http` package, this router supports variables in the routing pattern and matches against the request method. It also scales better.\n6: \n7: The router is optimized for high performance and a small memory footprint. It scales well even with very long paths and a large number of routes. A compressing dynamic trie (radix tree) structure is used for efficient matching.\n8: \n9: ","endLine":9,"startLine":1},{"content":"279: \n280: But this approach sidesteps the strict core rules of this router to avoid routing problems.
